    function checkRateLimit(ip: string): boolean {в”¬ГЂ
      const now = Date.now();в”¬ГЂ
      const entry = rateLimitMap.get(ip);в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      if (!entry || now > entry.resetAt) {в”¬ГЂ

        return true;в”¬ГЂ

      if (entry.count >= RATE_LIMIT_MAX) {в”¬ГЂ
        return false;в”¬ГЂ
      }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      entry.count++;в”¬ГЂ
      return true;в”¬ГЂ

    // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------в”¬ГЂ
    const rateLimitMap = new Map<string, { count: number; resetAt: number }>();в”¬ГЂ
    const RATE_LIMIT_MAX = 5;в”¬ГЂ
    const RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS = 60 * 60 * 1000; // 1 horaв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
    function checkRateLimit(ip: string): boolean {в”¬ГЂ
      const now = Date.now();в”¬ГЂ
      const entry = rateLimitMap.get(ip);в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      if (!entry || now > entry.resetAt) {в”¬ГЂ
        rateLimitMap.set(ip, { count: 1, resetAt: now + RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS });в”¬ГЂ
        return true;в”¬ГЂ
      }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      if (entry.count >= RATE_LIMIT_MAX) {в”¬ГЂ
        return false;в”¬ГЂ
      }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      entry.count++;в”¬ГЂ
      return true;в”¬ГЂ
    }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ

    const rateLimitMap = new Map<string, { count: number; resetAt: number }>();в”¬ГЂ
    const RATE_LIMIT_MAX = 5;в”¬ГЂ
    const RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS = 60 * 60 * 1000; // 1 horaв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
    function checkRateLimit(ip: string): boolean {в”¬ГЂ
      const now = Date.now();в”¬ГЂ
      const entry = rateLimitMap.get(ip);в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      if (!entry || now > entry.resetAt) {в”¬ГЂ
        rateLimitMap.set(ip, { count: 1, resetAt: now + RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS });в”¬ГЂ
        return true;в”¬ГЂ
      }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      if (entry.count >= RATE_LIMIT_MAX) {в”¬ГЂ
        return false;в”¬ГЂ
      }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      entry.count++;в”¬ГЂ
      return true;в”¬ГЂ
    }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ

    const RATE_LIMIT_MAX = 5;в”¬ГЂ
    const RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS = 60 * 60 * 1000; // 1 horaв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
    function checkRateLimit(ip: string): boolean {в”¬ГЂ
      const now = Date.now();в”¬ГЂ
      const entry = rateLimitMap.get(ip);в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      if (!entry || now > entry.resetAt) {в”¬ГЂ
        rateLimitMap.set(ip, { count: 1, resetAt: now + RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS });в”¬ГЂ
        return true;в”¬ГЂ
      }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      if (entry.count >= RATE_LIMIT_MAX) {в”¬ГЂ
        return false;в”¬ГЂ
      }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      entry.count++;в”¬ГЂ
      return true;в”¬ГЂ
    }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ

    const RATE_LIMIT_MAX = 5;в”¬ГЂ
    const RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS = 60 * 60 * 1000; // 1 horaв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
    function checkRateLimit(ip: string): boolean {в”¬ГЂ
      const now = Date.now();в”¬ГЂ
      const entry = rateLimitMap.get(ip);в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      if (!entry || now > entry.resetAt) {в”¬ГЂ
        rateLimitMap.set(ip, { count: 1, resetAt: now + RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS });в”¬ГЂ
        return true;в”¬ГЂ
      }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      if (entry.count >= RATE_LIMIT_MAX) {в”¬ГЂ
        return false;в”¬ГЂ
      }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      entry.count++;в”¬ГЂ
      return true;в”¬ГЂ
    }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ

    // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------в”¬ГЂ
    // Rate limit em memв”њв”‚ria (por IP, janela de 1h)в”¬ГЂ
    // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------в”¬ГЂ
    const rateLimitMap = new Map<string, { count: number; resetAt: number }>();в”¬ГЂ
    const RATE_LIMIT_MAX = 5;в”¬ГЂ
    const RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS = 60 * 60 * 1000; // 1 horaв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
    function checkRateLimit(ip: string): boolean {в”¬ГЂ
      const now = Date.now();в”¬ГЂ
      const entry = rateLimitMap.get(ip);в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      if (!entry || now > entry.resetAt) {в”¬ГЂ
        rateLimitMap.set(ip, { count: 1, resetAt: now + RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS });в”¬ГЂ
        return true;в”¬ГЂ
      }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      if (entry.count >= RATE_LIMIT_MAX) {в”¬ГЂ
        return false;в”¬ГЂ
      }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      entry.count++;в”¬ГЂ
      return true;в”¬ГЂ
    }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ

    // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------в”¬ГЂ
    const rateLimitMap = new Map<string, { count: number; resetAt: number }>();в”¬ГЂ
    const RATE_LIMIT_MAX = 5;в”¬ГЂ
    const RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS = 60 * 60 * 1000; // 1 horaв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
    function checkRateLimit(ip: string): boolean {в”¬ГЂ
      const now = Date.now();в”¬ГЂ
      const entry = rateLimitMap.get(ip);в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      if (!entry || now > entry.resetAt) {в”¬ГЂ
        rateLimitMap.set(ip, { count: 1, resetAt: now + RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS });в”¬ГЂ
        return true;в”¬ГЂ
      }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      if (entry.count >= RATE_LIMIT_MAX) {в”¬ГЂ
        return false;в”¬ГЂ
      }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      entry.count++;в”¬ГЂ
      return true;в”¬ГЂ
    }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ

    // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------в”¬ГЂ
    const rateLimitMap = new Map<string, { count: number; resetAt: number }>();в”¬ГЂ
    const RATE_LIMIT_MAX = 5;в”¬ГЂ
    const RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS = 60 * 60 * 1000; // 1 horaв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
    function checkRateLimit(ip: string): boolean {в”¬ГЂ
      const now = Date.now();в”¬ГЂ
      const entry = rateLimitMap.get(ip);в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      if (!entry || now > entry.resetAt) {в”¬ГЂ
        rateLimitMap.set(ip, { count: 1, resetAt: now + RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS });в”¬ГЂ
        return true;в”¬ГЂ
      }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      if (entry.count >= RATE_LIMIT_MAX) {в”¬ГЂ
        return false;в”¬ГЂ
      }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      entry.count++;в”¬ГЂ
      return true;в”¬ГЂ
    }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ

    // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------в”¬ГЂ
    // Rate limit em memв”њв”‚ria (por IP, janela de 1h)в”¬ГЂ
    // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------в”¬ГЂ
    const rateLimitMap = new Map<string, { count: number; resetAt: number }>();в”¬ГЂ
    const RATE_LIMIT_MAX = 5;в”¬ГЂ
    const RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS = 60 * 60 * 1000; // 1 horaв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
    function checkRateLimit(ip: string): boolean {в”¬ГЂ
      const now = Date.now();в”¬ГЂ
      const entry = rateLimitMap.get(ip);в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      if (!entry || now > entry.resetAt) {в”¬ГЂ
        rateLimitMap.set(ip, { count: 1, resetAt: now + RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS });в”¬ГЂ
        return true;в”¬ГЂ
      }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      if (entry.count >= RATE_LIMIT_MAX) {в”¬ГЂ
        return false;в”¬ГЂ
      }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      entry.count++;в”¬ГЂ
      return true;в”¬ГЂ
    }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ

     * Aceita multipart/form-data com dados pessoais + upload de documentos.в”¬ГЂ
     *в”¬ГЂ
     * PF: arquivo de CPF obrigatв”њв”‚rioв”¬ГЂ
     * PJ: cartв”њГєo CNPJ + CPF do responsв”њГ­vel obrigatв”њв”‚riosв”¬ГЂ
     *в”¬ГЂ
     * Rate limit: 5 cadastros/hora por IPв”¬ГЂ
     * Honeypot: campo \"website\" deve estar vazio (anti-bot)в”¬ГЂ
     */в”¬ГЂ
    import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';в”¬ГЂ
    import { query } from '@/lib/db';в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
    // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------в”¬ГЂ
    // CORS Г”Г‡Г¶ permite requisiв”њВєв”њГЃes da landing page (qwork.app.br) e do prв”њв”‚prio appв”¬ГЂ
    // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------в”¬ГЂ
    const ALLOWED_ORIGINS = [в”¬ГЂ
      'https://www.qwork.app.br',в”¬ГЂ
      'https://qwork.app.br',в”¬ГЂ
      process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_APP_URL,в”¬ГЂ
      process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_BASE_URL,в”¬ГЂ
    ].filter(Boolean) as string[];в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
    function getCorsHeaders(origin: string | null): HeadersInit {в”¬ГЂ
      const allowed =в”¬ГЂ
        origin && ALLOWED_ORIGINS.includes(origin) ? origin : ALLOWED_ORIGINS[0];в”¬ГЂ
      return {в”¬ГЂ
        'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': allowed,в”¬ГЂ
        'Access-Control-Allow-Methods': 'POST, OPTIONS',в”¬ГЂ
        'Access-Control-Allow-Headers': 'Content-Type',в”¬ГЂ
        'Access-Control-Max-Age': '86400',в”¬ГЂ
      };в”¬ГЂ
    }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
    /** Preflight OPTIONS para CORS */в”¬ГЂ
    export function OPTIONS(request: NextRequest): NextResponse {в”¬ГЂ
      const origin = request.headers.get('origin');в”¬ГЂ
      return new NextResponse(null, {в”¬ГЂ
        status: 204,в”¬ГЂ
        headers: getCorsHeaders(origin),в”¬ГЂ
      });в”¬ГЂ
    }в”¬ГЂ
    import {в”¬ГЂ
      validarCPF,в”¬ГЂ
      validarCNPJ,в”¬ГЂ
      validarEmail,в”¬ГЂ
      sanitizarString,в”¬ГЂ
      limparNumeros,в”¬ГЂ
      processarDocumentosUpload,в”¬ГЂ
    } from './helpers';в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
    export const dynamic = 'force-dynamic';в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
    // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------в”¬ГЂ
    // Rate limit em memв”њв”‚ria (por IP, janela de 1h)в”¬ГЂ
    // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------в”¬ГЂ
    const rateLimitMap = new Map<string, { count: number; resetAt: number }>();в”¬ГЂ
    const RATE_LIMIT_MAX = 5;в”¬ГЂ
    const RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS = 60 * 60 * 1000; // 1 horaв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
    function checkRateLimit(ip: string): boolean {в”¬ГЂ
      const now = Date.now();в”¬ГЂ
      const entry = rateLimitMap.get(ip);в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      if (!entry || now > entry.resetAt) {в”¬ГЂ
        rateLimitMap.set(ip, { count: 1, resetAt: now + RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS });в”¬ГЂ
        return true;в”¬ГЂ
      }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      if (entry.count >= RATE_LIMIT_MAX) {в”¬ГЂ
        return false;в”¬ГЂ
      }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      entry.count++;в”¬ГЂ
      return true;в”¬ГЂ
    }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
    export async function POST(request: NextRequest): Promise<NextResponse> {в”¬ГЂ
      try {в”¬ГЂ
        // 1. Rate limit por IPв”¬ГЂ
        const ip =в”¬ГЂ
          request.headers.get('x-forwarded-for')?.split(',')[0]?.trim() ||в”¬ГЂ
          request.headers.get('x-real-ip') ||в”¬ГЂ
          'unknown';в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
        if (!checkRateLimit(ip)) {в”¬ГЂ
          return NextResponse.json(в”¬ГЂ
            {в”¬ГЂ
              success: false,в”¬ГЂ
              error: 'Muitas tentativas. Aguarde 1 hora antes de tentar novamente.',в”¬ГЂ
              code: 'RATE_LIMIT',в”¬ГЂ
            },в”¬ГЂ
            { status: 429 }в”¬ГЂ
          );в”¬ГЂ
        }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
        // 2. Parsear FormDataв”¬ГЂ
        let formData: FormData;в”¬ГЂ
        try {в”¬ГЂ
          formData = await request.formData();в”¬ГЂ
        } catch {в”¬ГЂ
          return NextResponse.json(в”¬ГЂ
            {в”¬ГЂ
              success: false,в”¬ГЂ
              error: 'Envie os dados como multipart/form-data',в”¬ГЂ
              code: 'INVALID_FORMAT',в”¬ГЂ
            },в”¬ГЂ
            { status: 400 }в”¬ГЂ
          );в”¬ГЂ
        }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
        // 3. Honeypot checkв”¬ГЂ
        const honeypot = (formData.get('website') as string) ?? '';в”¬ГЂ
        if (honeypot.length > 0) {в”¬ГЂ
          // Bot detectado Г”Г‡Г¶ retorna sucesso falsoв”¬ГЂ
          return NextResponse.json({в”¬ГЂ
            success: true,в”¬ГЂ
            id: 'ok',в”¬ГЂ
            status: 'pendente_verificacao',в”¬ГЂ
          });в”¬ГЂ
        }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
        // 4. Extrair e validar campos comunsв”¬ГЂ
        const tipoPessoa = (formData.get('tipo_pessoa') as string)?.toLowerCase();в”¬ГЂ
        if (tipoPessoa !== 'pf' && tipoPessoa !== 'pj') {в”¬ГЂ
          return NextResponse.json(в”¬ГЂ
            {в”¬ГЂ
              success: false,в”¬ГЂ
              error: 'tipo_pessoa deve ser PF ou PJ',в”¬ГЂ
              field: 'tipo_pessoa',в”¬ГЂ
              code: 'VALIDATION',в”¬ГЂ
            },в”¬ГЂ
            { status: 400 }в”¬ГЂ
          );в”¬ГЂ
        }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
        const nome = sanitizarString((formData.get('nome') as string) ?? '');в”¬ГЂ
        if (!nome || nome.length < 3 || nome.length > 200) {в”¬ГЂ
          return NextResponse.json(в”¬ГЂ
            {в”¬ГЂ
              success: false,в”¬ГЂ
              error: 'Nome deve ter entre 3 e 200 caracteres',в”¬ГЂ
              field: 'nome',в”¬ГЂ
              code: 'VALIDATION',в”¬ГЂ
            },в”¬ГЂ
            { status: 400 }в”¬ГЂ
          );в”¬ГЂ
        }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
        const email = ((formData.get('email') as string) ?? '')в”¬ГЂ
          .trim()в”¬ГЂ
          .toLowerCase();в”¬ГЂ
        if (!validarEmail(email)) {в”¬ГЂ
          return NextResponse.json(в”¬ГЂ
            {в”¬ГЂ
              success: false,в”¬ГЂ
              error: 'E-mail invв”њГ­lido',в”¬ГЂ
              field: 'email',в”¬ГЂ
              code: 'VALIDATION',в”¬ГЂ
            },в”¬ГЂ
            { status: 400 }в”¬ГЂ
          );в”¬ГЂ
        }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
        const telefone = limparNumeros((formData.get('telefone') as string) ?? '');в”¬ГЂ
        if (telefone.length < 10 || telefone.length > 11) {в”¬ГЂ
          return NextResponse.json(в”¬ГЂ
            {в”¬ГЂ
              success: false,в”¬ГЂ
              error: 'Telefone invв”њГ­lido (DDD + nв”њв•‘mero)',в”¬ГЂ
              field: 'telefone',в”¬ГЂ
              code: 'VALIDATION',в”¬ГЂ
            },в”¬ГЂ
            { status: 400 }в”¬ГЂ
          );в”¬ГЂ
        }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
        // 5. Validar campos especв”њВЎficos por tipo de pessoaв”¬ГЂ
        let cpf: string | null = null;в”¬ГЂ
        let cnpj: string | null = null;в”¬ГЂ
        let razaoSocial: string | null = null;в”¬ГЂ
        let cpfResponsavel: string | null = null;в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
        if (tipoPessoa === 'pf') {в”¬ГЂ
          cpf = limparNumeros((formData.get('cpf') as string) ?? '');в”¬ГЂ
          if (!validarCPF(cpf)) {в”¬ГЂ
            return NextResponse.json(в”¬ГЂ
              {в”¬ГЂ
                success: false,в”¬ГЂ
                error: 'CPF invв”њГ­lido',в”¬ГЂ
                field: 'cpf',в”¬ГЂ
                code: 'VALIDATION',в”¬ГЂ
              },в”¬ГЂ
              { status: 400 }в”¬ГЂ
            );в”¬ГЂ
          }в”¬ГЂ
        } else {в”¬ГЂ
          cnpj = limparNumeros((formData.get('cnpj') as string) ?? '');в”¬ГЂ
          if (!validarCNPJ(cnpj)) {в”¬ГЂ
            return NextResponse.json(в”¬ГЂ
              {в”¬ГЂ
                success: false,в”¬ГЂ
                error: 'CNPJ invв”њГ­lido',в”¬ГЂ
                field: 'cnpj',в”¬ГЂ
                code: 'VALIDATION',в”¬ГЂ
              },в”¬ГЂ
              { status: 400 }в”¬ГЂ
            );в”¬ГЂ
          }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
          razaoSocial = sanitizarString(в”¬ГЂ
            (formData.get('razao_social') as string) ?? ''в”¬ГЂ
          );в”¬ГЂ
          if (!razaoSocial || razaoSocial.length < 3) {в”¬ГЂ
            return NextResponse.json(в”¬ГЂ
              {в”¬ГЂ
                success: false,в”¬ГЂ
                error: 'Razв”њГєo social obrigatв”њв”‚ria para PJ',в”¬ГЂ
                field: 'razao_social',в”¬ГЂ
                code: 'VALIDATION',в”¬ГЂ
              },в”¬ГЂ
              { status: 400 }в”¬ГЂ
            );в”¬ГЂ
          }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
          cpfResponsavel = limparNumeros(в”¬ГЂ
            (formData.get('cpf_responsavel') as string) ?? ''в”¬ГЂ
          );в”¬ГЂ
          if (!validarCPF(cpfResponsavel)) {в”¬ГЂ
            return NextResponse.json(в”¬ГЂ
              {в”¬ГЂ
                success: false,в”¬ГЂ
                error: 'CPF do responsв”њГ­vel invв”њГ­lido',в”¬ГЂ
                field: 'cpf_responsavel',в”¬ГЂ
                code: 'VALIDATION',в”¬ГЂ
              },в”¬ГЂ
              { status: 400 }в”¬ГЂ
            );в”¬ГЂ
          }в”¬ГЂ
        }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
        // 6. Verificar duplicatas no banco (apenas leads nв”њГєo rejeitados)в”¬ГЂ
        const emailExists = await query(в”¬ГЂ
          `SELECT id FROM representantes_cadastro_leads WHERE email = $1 AND status NOT IN ('rejeitado')`,в”¬ГЂ
          [email]в”¬ГЂ
        );в”¬ГЂ
        if (emailExists.rows.length > 0) {в”¬ГЂ
          return NextResponse.json(в”¬ГЂ
            {в”¬ГЂ
              success: false,в”¬ГЂ
              error: 'Este e-mail jв”њГ­ possui um cadastro em anв”њГ­lise',в”¬ГЂ
              field: 'email',в”¬ГЂ
              code: 'DUPLICATE',в”¬ГЂ
            },в”¬ГЂ
            { status: 409 }в”¬ГЂ
          );в”¬ГЂ
        }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
        // Verificar duplicata tambв”њВ®m na tabela de representantes oficiaisв”¬ГЂ
        const emailExistsRep = await query(в”¬ГЂ
          `SELECT id FROM representantes WHERE email = $1`,в”¬ГЂ
          [email]в”¬ГЂ
        );в”¬ГЂ
        if (emailExistsRep.rows.length > 0) {в”¬ГЂ
          return NextResponse.json(в”¬ГЂ
            {в”¬ГЂ
              success: false,в”¬ГЂ
              error: 'Este e-mail jв”њГ­ estв”њГ­ cadastrado como representante',в”¬ГЂ
              field: 'email',в”¬ГЂ
              code: 'DUPLICATE',в”¬ГЂ
            },в”¬ГЂ
            { status: 409 }в”¬ГЂ
          );в”¬ГЂ
        }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
        if (tipoPessoa === 'pf' && cpf) {в”¬ГЂ
          const cpfExists = await query(в”¬ГЂ
            `SELECT id FROM representantes_cadastro_leads WHERE cpf = $1 AND status NOT IN ('rejeitado')`,в”¬ГЂ
            [cpf]в”¬ГЂ
          );в”¬ГЂ
          if (cpfExists.rows.length > 0) {в”¬ГЂ
            return NextResponse.json(в”¬ГЂ
              {в”¬ГЂ
                success: false,в”¬ГЂ
                error: 'Este CPF jв”њГ­ possui um cadastro em anв”њГ­lise',в”¬ГЂ
                field: 'cpf',в”¬ГЂ
                code: 'DUPLICATE',в”¬ГЂ
              },в”¬ГЂ
              { status: 409 }в”¬ГЂ
            );в”¬ГЂ
          }в”¬ГЂ
          const cpfExistsRep = await query(в”¬ГЂ
            `SELECT id FROM representantes WHERE cpf = $1`,в”¬ГЂ
            [cpf]в”¬ГЂ
          );в”¬ГЂ
          if (cpfExistsRep.rows.length > 0) {в”¬ГЂ
            return NextResponse.json(в”¬ГЂ
              {в”¬ГЂ
                success: false,в”¬ГЂ
                error: 'Este CPF jв”њГ­ estв”њГ­ cadastrado como representante',в”¬ГЂ
                field: 'cpf',в”¬ГЂ
                code: 'DUPLICATE',в”¬ГЂ
              },в”¬ГЂ
              { status: 409 }в”¬ГЂ
            );в”¬ГЂ
          }в”¬ГЂ
        }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
        if (tipoPessoa === 'pj' && cnpj) {в”¬ГЂ
          const cnpjExists = await query(в”¬ГЂ
            `SELECT id FROM representantes_cadastro_leads WHERE cnpj = $1 AND status NOT IN ('rejeitado')`,в”¬ГЂ
            [cnpj]в”¬ГЂ
          );в”¬ГЂ
          if (cnpjExists.rows.length > 0) {в”¬ГЂ
            return NextResponse.json(в”¬ГЂ
              {в”¬ГЂ
                success: false,в”¬ГЂ
                error: 'Este CNPJ jв”њГ­ possui um cadastro em anв”њГ­lise',в”¬ГЂ
                field: 'cnpj',в”¬ГЂ
                code: 'DUPLICATE',в”¬ГЂ
              },в”¬ГЂ
              { status: 409 }в”¬ГЂ
            );в”¬ГЂ
          }в”¬ГЂ
          const cnpjExistsRep = await query(в”¬ГЂ
            `SELECT id FROM representantes WHERE cnpj = $1`,в”¬ГЂ
            [cnpj]в”¬ГЂ
          );в”¬ГЂ
          if (cnpjExistsRep.rows.length > 0) {в”¬ГЂ
            return NextResponse.json(в”¬ГЂ
              {в”¬ГЂ
                success: false,в”¬ГЂ
                error: 'Este CNPJ jв”њГ­ estв”њГ­ cadastrado como representante',в”¬ГЂ
                field: 'cnpj',в”¬ГЂ
                code: 'DUPLICATE',в”¬ГЂ
              },в”¬ГЂ
              { status: 409 }в”¬ГЂ
            );в”¬ГЂ
          }в”¬ГЂ
        }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
        // 7. Validar e processar arquivosв”¬ГЂ
        const identificador = tipoPessoa === 'pf' ? cpf! : cnpj!;в”¬ГЂ
        const { docs: docsUpload, error: docError } =в”¬ГЂ
          await processarDocumentosUpload(formData, tipoPessoa, identificador);в”¬ГЂ
        if (docError) return docError;в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
        // 8. Inserir no bancoв”¬ГЂ
        const docCpfData = docsUpload.find((d) => d.tipo === 'cpf');в”¬ГЂ
        const docCnpjData = docsUpload.find((d) => d.tipo === 'cnpj');в”¬ГЂ
        const docCpfRespData = docsUpload.find((d) => d.tipo === 'cpf_responsavel');в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
        const userAgent = request.headers.get('user-agent') ?? '';в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
        const insertResult = await query<{ id: string }>(в”¬ГЂ
          `INSERT INTO representantes_cadastro_leads (в”¬ГЂ
            tipo_pessoa, nome, email, telefone,в”¬ГЂ
            cpf, cnpj, razao_social, cpf_responsavel,в”¬ГЂ
            doc_cpf_filename, doc_cpf_key, doc_cpf_url,в”¬ГЂ
            doc_cnpj_filename, doc_cnpj_key, doc_cnpj_url,в”¬ГЂ

            ip_origem, user_agentв”¬ГЂ
          ) VALUES (в”¬ГЂ
            $1, $2, $3, $4,в”¬ГЂ
            $5, $6, $7, $8,в”¬ГЂ
            $9, $10, $11,в”¬ГЂ
            $12, $13, $14,в”¬ГЂ
            $15, $16, $17,в”¬ГЂ
            $18, $19в”¬ГЂ
          ) RETURNING id`,в”¬ГЂ
          [в”¬ГЂ
            tipoPessoa,в”¬ГЂ
            nome,в”¬ГЂ
            email,в”¬ГЂ
            telefone,в”¬ГЂ
            cpf,в”¬ГЂ
            cnpj,в”¬ГЂ
            razaoSocial,в”¬ГЂ
            cpfResponsavel,в”¬ГЂ
            docCpfData?.filename ?? null,в”¬ГЂ
            docCpfData?.key ?? null,в”¬ГЂ
            docCpfData?.url ?? null,в”¬ГЂ
            docCnpjData?.filename ?? null,в”¬ГЂ
            docCnpjData?.key ?? null,в”¬ГЂ
            docCnpjData?.url ?? null,в”¬ГЂ
            docCpfRespData?.filename ?? null,в”¬ГЂ
            docCpfRespData?.key ?? null,в”¬ГЂ
            docCpfRespData?.url ?? null,в”¬ГЂ
            ip,в”¬ГЂ
            userAgent,в”¬ГЂ
          ]в”¬ГЂ
        );в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
        const leadId = insertResult.rows[0]?.id;в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
        console.log(в”¬ГЂ
          `[CADASTRO-REP] Novo lead criado: ${leadId} Г”Г‡Г¶ ${tipoPessoa.toUpperCase()} Г”Г‡Г¶ ${nome} Г”Г‡Г¶ ${email}`в”¬ГЂ
        );в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
        // 9. Notificar usuв”њГ­rios comercial sobre novo cadastro de representanteв”¬ГЂ
        try {в”¬ГЂ
          const comercialUsers = await query<{ id: number; nome: string }>(в”¬ГЂ
            `SELECT id, nome FROM usuarios WHERE tipo_usuario = 'comercial' AND ativo = true`в”¬ГЂ
          );в”¬ГЂ
          if (comercialUsers.rows.length > 0) {в”¬ГЂ
            // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-unused-varsв”¬ГЂ
            const _notifValues = comercialUsers.rowsв”¬ГЂ
              .map(в”¬ГЂ
                (_, idx) =>в”¬ГЂ
                  `($${idx * 6 + 1}, $${idx * 6 + 2}, $${idx * 6 + 3}, $${idx * 6 + 4}, $${idx * 6 + 5}, $${idx * 6 + 6})`в”¬ГЂ
              )в”¬ГЂ
              .join(', ');в”¬ГЂ
            const notifParams = comercialUsers.rows.flatMap((u) => [в”¬ГЂ
              'novo_cadastro_representante',в”¬ГЂ
              u.id,в”¬ГЂ
              'comercial',в”¬ГЂ
              'Novo cadastro de representante',в”¬ГЂ
              `${tipoPessoa === 'pf' ? nome : (razaoSocial ?? nome)} solicitou cadastro como representante. Clique para analisar.`,в”¬ГЂ
              `/comercial/representantes/cadastros/${leadId}`,в”¬ГЂ
            ]);в”¬ГЂ
            await query(в”¬ГЂ
              `INSERT INTO notificacoes (tipo, destinatario_id, destinatario_tipo, titulo, mensagem, link_acao, created_at)в”¬ГЂ
               VALUES ${comercialUsers.rows.map((_, idx) => `($${idx * 6 + 1}, $${idx * 6 + 2}, $${idx * 6 + 3}, $${idx * 6 + 4}, $${idx * 6 + 5}, $${idx * 6 + 6}, NOW())`).join(', ')}`,в”¬ГЂ
              notifParamsв”¬ГЂ
            );в”¬ГЂ
          }в”¬ГЂ
          console.log(в”¬ГЂ
            `[NOTIF-COMERCIAL] ${comercialUsers.rows.length} notificaв”њВєв”њГєo(в”њГЃes) criada(s) para lead ${leadId}`в”¬ГЂ
          );в”¬ГЂ

    // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------в”¬ГЂ
    const rateLimitMap = new Map<string, { count: number; resetAt: number }>();в”¬ГЂ
    const RATE_LIMIT_MAX = 5;в”¬ГЂ
    const RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS = 60 * 60 * 1000; // 1 horaв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
    function checkRateLimit(ip: string): boolean {в”¬ГЂ
      const now = Date.now();в”¬ГЂ
      const entry = rateLimitMap.get(ip);в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      if (!entry || now > entry.resetAt) {в”¬ГЂ
        rateLimitMap.set(ip, { count: 1, resetAt: now + RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS });в”¬ГЂ
        return true;в”¬ГЂ
      }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      if (entry.count >= RATE_LIMIT_MAX) {в”¬ГЂ
        return false;в”¬ГЂ
      }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      entry.count++;в”¬ГЂ
      return true;в”¬ГЂ
    }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ

    // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------в”¬ГЂ
    const rateLimitMap = new Map<string, { count: number; resetAt: number }>();в”¬ГЂ
    const RATE_LIMIT_MAX = 5;в”¬ГЂ
    const RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS = 60 * 60 * 1000; // 1 horaв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
    function checkRateLimit(ip: string): boolean {в”¬ГЂ
      const now = Date.now();в”¬ГЂ
      const entry = rateLimitMap.get(ip);в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      if (!entry || now > entry.resetAt) {в”¬ГЂ
        rateLimitMap.set(ip, { count: 1, resetAt: now + RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS });в”¬ГЂ
        return true;в”¬ГЂ
      }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      if (entry.count >= RATE_LIMIT_MAX) {в”¬ГЂ
        return false;в”¬ГЂ
      }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      entry.count++;в”¬ГЂ
      return true;в”¬ГЂ
    }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ

    // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------в”¬ГЂ
    const rateLimitMap = new Map<string, { count: number; resetAt: number }>();в”¬ГЂ
    const RATE_LIMIT_MAX = 5;в”¬ГЂ
    const RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS = 60 * 60 * 1000; // 1 horaв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
    function checkRateLimit(ip: string): boolean {в”¬ГЂ
      const now = Date.now();в”¬ГЂ
      const entry = rateLimitMap.get(ip);в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      if (!entry || now > entry.resetAt) {в”¬ГЂ
        rateLimitMap.set(ip, { count: 1, resetAt: now + RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS });в”¬ГЂ
        return true;в”¬ГЂ
      }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      if (entry.count >= RATE_LIMIT_MAX) {в”¬ГЂ
        return false;в”¬ГЂ
      }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      entry.count++;в”¬ГЂ
      return true;в”¬ГЂ
    }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ

    const RATE_LIMIT_MAX = 5;в”¬ГЂ
    const RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS = 60 * 60 * 1000; // 1 horaв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
    function checkRateLimit(ip: string): boolean {в”¬ГЂ
      const now = Date.now();в”¬ГЂ
      const entry = rateLimitMap.get(ip);в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      if (!entry || now > entry.resetAt) {в”¬ГЂ
        rateLimitMap.set(ip, { count: 1, resetAt: now + RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS });в”¬ГЂ
        return true;в”¬ГЂ
      }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      if (entry.count >= RATE_LIMIT_MAX) {в”¬ГЂ
        return false;в”¬ГЂ
      }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      entry.count++;в”¬ГЂ
      return true;в”¬ГЂ
    }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ

    // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------в”¬ГЂ
    const rateLimitMap = new Map<string, { count: number; resetAt: number }>();в”¬ГЂ
    const RATE_LIMIT_MAX = 5;в”¬ГЂ
    const RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS = 60 * 60 * 1000; // 1 horaв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
    function checkRateLimit(ip: string): boolean {в”¬ГЂ
      const now = Date.now();в”¬ГЂ
      const entry = rateLimitMap.get(ip);в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      if (!entry || now > entry.resetAt) {в”¬ГЂ
        rateLimitMap.set(ip, { count: 1, resetAt: now + RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS });в”¬ГЂ
        return true;в”¬ГЂ
      }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      if (entry.count >= RATE_LIMIT_MAX) {в”¬ГЂ
        return false;в”¬ГЂ
      }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
      entry.count++;в”¬ГЂ
      return true;в”¬ГЂ
    }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ

    // Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡ Handler Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
    export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {в”¬ГЂ
      try {в”¬ГЂ
        // Isola a falha de parse (ex.: body sem boundary multipart) como 400,в”¬ГЂ
        // evitando que vire Unexpected error 500.в”¬ГЂ
        let formData: FormData;в”¬ГЂ
        try {в”¬ГЂ
          formData = await req.formData();в”¬ГЂ
        } catch {в”¬ГЂ
          return NextResponse.json(в”¬ГЂ
            { errors: { form: \"Formato de envio invв”њГ­lido. Tente novamente.\" } },в”¬ГЂ
            { status: 400 },в”¬ГЂ
          );в”¬ГЂ
        }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
        // Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡ Honeypot Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡в”¬ГЂ
        const honeypot = formData.get(\"website\") as string | null;в”¬ГЂ
        if (honeypot) {в”¬ГЂ
          // Bot detected Г”Г‡Г¶ retorna 200 silenciosoв”¬ГЂ
          return NextResponse.json({ ok: true }, { status: 200 });в”¬ГЂ
        }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
        // Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡ Extrair campos de texto Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡в”¬ГЂ
        const tipoPessoa = formData.get(\"tipoPessoa\") as string;в”¬ГЂ
        const nome = formData.get(\"nome\") as string;в”¬ГЂ
        const email = formData.get(\"email\") as string;в”¬ГЂ
        const telefone = formData.get(\"telefone\") as string;в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
        const raw: Record<string, string> = {в”¬ГЂ
          tipoPessoa,в”¬ГЂ
          nome: nome ?? \"\",в”¬ГЂ
          email: email ?? \"\",в”¬ГЂ
          telefone: telefone ?? \"\",в”¬ГЂ
          website: \"\",в”¬ГЂ
        };в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
        if (tipoPessoa === \"PF\") {в”¬ГЂ
          raw.cpf = (formData.get(\"cpf\") as string) ?? \"\";в”¬ГЂ
        } else if (tipoPessoa === \"PJ\") {в”¬ГЂ
          raw.razaoSocial = (formData.get(\"razaoSocial\") as string) ?? \"\";в”¬ГЂ
          raw.cnpj = (formData.get(\"cnpj\") as string) ?? \"\";в”¬ГЂ
          raw.cpfResponsavel = (formData.get(\"cpfResponsavel\") as string) ?? \"\";в”¬ГЂ
        } else {в”¬ГЂ
          return NextResponse.json(в”¬ГЂ
            { errors: { tipoPessoa: \"Tipo de pessoa invв”њГ­lido.\" } },в”¬ГЂ
            { status: 400 },в”¬ГЂ
          );в”¬ГЂ
        }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
        // Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡ Validaв”њВєв”њГєo Zod Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡в”¬ГЂ
        const schema =в”¬ГЂ
          tipoPessoa === \"PF\" ? pessoaFisicaSchema : pessoaJuridicaSchema;в”¬ГЂ
        const result = schema.safeParse(raw);в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
        if (!result.success) {в”¬ГЂ
          return NextResponse.json(в”¬ГЂ
            { errors: fieldErrors(result.error.issues) },в”¬ГЂ
            { status: 400 },в”¬ГЂ
          );в”¬ГЂ
        }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
        // Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡ Validar arquivos Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡в”¬ГЂ
        const fileErrors: Record<string, string> = {};в”¬ГЂ
        let hasFiles = false;в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
        if (tipoPessoa === \"PF\") {в”¬ГЂ
          const docCpf = formData.get(\"documentoCpf\") as File | null;в”¬ГЂ
          if (docCpf && docCpf.size > 0) {в”¬ГЂ
            const v = validateFile(docCpf);в”¬ГЂ
            if (!v.valid) fileErrors.documentoCpf = v.error;в”¬ГЂ
            else hasFiles = true;в”¬ГЂ
          }в”¬ГЂ
        } else {в”¬ГЂ
          const docCnpj = formData.get(\"documentoCnpj\") as File | null;в”¬ГЂ
          const docCpfResp = formData.get(\"documentoCpfResponsavel\") as File | null;в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
          if (docCnpj && docCnpj.size > 0) {в”¬ГЂ
            const v = validateFile(docCnpj);в”¬ГЂ
            if (!v.valid) fileErrors.documentoCnpj = v.error;в”¬ГЂ
            else hasFiles = true;в”¬ГЂ
          }в”¬ГЂ
          if (docCpfResp && docCpfResp.size > 0) {в”¬ГЂ
            const v = validateFile(docCpfResp);в”¬ГЂ
            if (!v.valid) fileErrors.documentoCpfResponsavel = v.error;в”¬ГЂ
            else hasFiles = true;в”¬ГЂ
          }в”¬ГЂ
        }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
        if (Object.keys(fileErrors).length > 0) {в”¬ГЂ
          return NextResponse.json({ errors: fileErrors }, { status: 400 });в”¬ГЂ
        }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
        // Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡ Upload Backblaze (staging/prod Г”Г‡Г¶ VERCEL=1) Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡в”¬ГЂ
        // Em DEV o backend QWork faz o upload; no Vercel a LP sobe diretamente.в”¬ГЂ
        // Se credenciais nв”њГєo existem Г”Г‡Г¶ fallback para delegaв”њВєв”њГєo ao QWork.в”¬ГЂ
        const isVercel = process.env.VERCEL === \"1\";в”¬ГЂ
        const backblazeUploads: Record<string, DocUploadResult> = {};в”¬ГЂ
        let backblazeCredentialsMissing = false;в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
        if (isVercel) {в”¬ГЂ
          const { uploadDocumentoRepresentante } =в”¬ГЂ
            await import(\"@/lib/storage/representante-storage\");в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
          // Identificador somente dв”њВЎgitos (CPF para PF, CNPJ para PJ)в”¬ГЂ
          const identificador =в”¬ГЂ
            tipoPessoa === \"PF\"в”¬ГЂ
              ? (raw.cpf ?? \"\").replace(/\\D/g, \"\")в”¬ГЂ
              : (raw.cnpj ?? \"\").replace(/\\D/g, \"\");в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
          try {в”¬ГЂ
            if (tipoPessoa === \"PF\") {в”¬ГЂ
              const docCpf = formData.get(\"documentoCpf\") as File | null;в”¬ГЂ
              if (docCpf && docCpf.size > 0) {в”¬ГЂ
                console.log(в”¬ГЂ
                  `[REPRESENTANTE] Upload PF: documentoCpf (${docCpf.size} bytes, ${docCpf.type})`,в”¬ГЂ
                );в”¬ГЂ
                backblazeUploads.cpf = await uploadDocumentoRepresentante(в”¬ГЂ
                  docCpf,в”¬ГЂ
                  \"cpf\",в”¬ГЂ
                  identificador,в”¬ГЂ
                  \"PF\",в”¬ГЂ
                );в”¬ГЂ
              }в”¬ГЂ
            } else {в”¬ГЂ
              const docCnpj = formData.get(\"documentoCnpj\") as File | null;в”¬ГЂ

                \"documentoCpfResponsavel\",в”¬ГЂ

                );в”¬ГЂ
                backblazeUploads.cnpj = await uploadDocumentoRepresentante(в”¬ГЂ
                  docCnpj,в”¬ГЂ
                  \"cnpj\",в”¬ГЂ
                  identificador,в”¬ГЂ
                  \"PJ\",в”¬ГЂ
                );в”¬ГЂ
              }в”¬ГЂ
              if (docCpfResp && docCpfResp.size > 0) {в”¬ГЂ
                console.log(в”¬ГЂ
                  `[REPRESENTANTE] Upload PJ: documentoCpfResponsavel (${docCpfResp.size} bytes, ${docCpfResp.type})`,в”¬ГЂ
                );в”¬ГЂ
                backblazeUploads.cpf_responsavel =в”¬ГЂ
                  await uploadDocumentoRepresentante(в”¬ГЂ
                    docCpfResp,в”¬ГЂ
                    \"cpf_responsavel\",в”¬ГЂ
                    identificador,в”¬ГЂ
                    \"PJ\",в”¬ГЂ
                  );в”¬ГЂ
              }в”¬ГЂ
            }в”¬ГЂ
          } catch (uploadErr) {в”¬ГЂ
            const errMsg =в”¬ГЂ
              uploadErr instanceof Error ? uploadErr.message : String(uploadErr);в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
            // Se credenciais nв”њГєo configuradas Г”Г‡Г¶ fallback para DEV mode (repassa ao QWork)в”¬ГЂ
            if (в”¬ГЂ
              (uploadErr as any)?.code === \"BACKBLAZE_CREDENTIALS_MISSING\" ||в”¬ГЂ
              errMsg.includes(\"Credenciais nв”њГєo configuradas\")в”¬ГЂ
            ) {в”¬ГЂ
              console.warn(в”¬ГЂ
                \"[REPRESENTANTE] Credenciais Backblaze nв”њГєo configuradas Г”Г‡Г¶ fallback para DEV mode (QWork farв”њГ­ upload)\",в”¬ГЂ
              );в”¬ГЂ
              backblazeCredentialsMissing = true;в”¬ГЂ
              // Continuar normalmente Г”Г‡Г¶ forwardData repassarв”њГ­ os arquivos ao QWorkв”¬ГЂ
            } else {в”¬ГЂ

                message: errMsg,в”¬ГЂ
                code: (uploadErr as any)?.Code || (uploadErr as any)?.code,в”¬ГЂ
                keyId: process.env.BACKBLAZE_REP_KEY_IDв”¬ГЂ
                  ? `${process.env.BACKBLAZE_REP_KEY_ID.slice(0, 10)}...`в”¬ГЂ
                  : process.env.BACKBLAZE_KEY_IDв”¬ГЂ
                    ? `${process.env.BACKBLAZE_KEY_ID.slice(0, 10)}... (fallback BACKBLAZE_KEY_ID)`в”¬ГЂ
                    : \"(nenhuma credencial encontrada)\",в”¬ГЂ
                endpoint: process.env.BACKBLAZE_ENDPOINT || \"(default)\",в”¬ГЂ
              });в”¬ГЂ
              return NextResponse.json(в”¬ГЂ
                { errors: { form: \"Erro ao enviar documentos. Tente novamente.\" } },в”¬ГЂ
                { status: 503 },в”¬ГЂ
              );в”¬ГЂ
            }в”¬ГЂ
          }в”¬ГЂ
        }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
        // Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡ Gerar token Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡в”¬ГЂ
        const token = crypto.randomUUID();в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
        // Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡ Encaminhar ao backend QWork Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡в”¬ГЂ
        // QWORK_API_SKIP=true permite testar a LP localmente sem o backend QWork.в”¬ГЂ
        // Em produв”њВєв”њГєo, mantenha QWORK_API_SKIP indefinido ou false.в”¬ГЂ
        const skipQWork = process.env.QWORK_API_SKIP === \"true\";в”¬ГЂ
        const qworkUrl = process.env.QWORK_API_URL || \"http://localhost:3001\";в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
        if (skipQWork) {в”¬ГЂ
          console.log(в”¬ГЂ
            \"[REPRESENTANTE][DEV] QWORK_API_SKIP=true Г”Г‡Г¶ encaminhamento ao QWork ignorado.\",в”¬ГЂ
            {в”¬ГЂ
              tipoPessoa: raw.tipoPessoa,в”¬ГЂ
              nome: raw.nome,в”¬ГЂ
              email: raw.email,в”¬ГЂ
              token,в”¬ГЂ
              hasFiles,в”¬ГЂ
            },в”¬ГЂ
          );в”¬ГЂ
        } else {в”¬ГЂ
          // Mapeia campos camelCase da LP para snake_case esperado pelo QWorkв”¬ГЂ
          const forwardData = new FormData();в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
          // Campos comunsв”¬ГЂ
          forwardData.append(\"tipo_pessoa\", (raw.tipoPessoa ?? \"\").toLowerCase());в”¬ГЂ
          forwardData.append(\"nome\", raw.nome ?? \"\");в”¬ГЂ

        // Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡ Validaв”њВєв”њГєo Zod Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡в”¬ГЂ
        const schema =в”¬ГЂ
          tipoPessoa === \"PF\" ? pessoaFisicaSchema : pessoaJuridicaSchema;в”¬ГЂ

        if (!result.success) {в”¬ГЂ

            { errors: fieldErrors(result.error.issues) },в”¬ГЂ
            { status: 400 },в”¬ГЂ
          );в”¬ГЂ
        }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
        // Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡ Validar arquivos Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡в”¬ГЂ
        const fileErrors: Record<string, string> = {};в”¬ГЂ
        let hasFiles = false;в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
        if (tipoPessoa === \"PF\") {в”¬ГЂ
          const docCpf = formData.get(\"documentoCpf\") as File | null;в”¬ГЂ
          if (docCpf && docCpf.size > 0) {в”¬ГЂ
            const v = validateFile(docCpf);в”¬ГЂ
            if (!v.valid) fileErrors.documentoCpf = v.error;в”¬ГЂ
            else hasFiles = true;в”¬ГЂ
          }в”¬ГЂ
        } else {в”¬ГЂ
          const docCnpj = formData.get(\"documentoCnpj\") as File | null;в”¬ГЂ

            const v = validateFile(docCnpj);в”¬ГЂ
            if (!v.valid) fileErrors.documentoCnpj = v.error;в”¬ГЂ
            else hasFiles = true;в”¬ГЂ
          }в”¬ГЂ
          if (docCpfResp && docCpfResp.size > 0) {в”¬ГЂ
            const v = validateFile(docCpfResp);в”¬ГЂ
            if (!v.valid) fileErrors.documentoCpfResponsavel = v.error;в”¬ГЂ
            else hasFiles = true;в”¬ГЂ
          }в”¬ГЂ
        }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
        if (Object.keys(fileErrors).length > 0) {в”¬ГЂ
          return NextResponse.json({ errors: fileErrors }, { status: 400 });в”¬ГЂ
        }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
        // Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡ Upload Backblaze (staging/prod Г”Г‡Г¶ VERCEL=1) Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡в”¬ГЂ
        // Em DEV o backend QWork faz o upload; no Vercel a LP sobe diretamente.в”¬ГЂ

            tipoPessoa === \"PF\"в”¬ГЂ
              ? (raw.cpf ?? \"\").replace(/\\D/g, \"\")в”¬ГЂ

                  docCpf,в”¬ГЂ

                  await uploadDocumentoRepresentante(в”¬ГЂ

                    \"PJ\",в”¬ГЂ

              }в”¬ГЂ
            }в”¬ГЂ
          } catch (uploadErr) {в”¬ГЂ

              uploadErr instanceof Error ? uploadErr.message : String(uploadErr);в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ

            } else {в”¬ГЂ

                keyId: process.env.BACKBLAZE_REP_KEY_IDв”¬ГЂ

                    ? `${process.env.BACKBLAZE_KEY_ID.slice(0, 10)}... (fallback BACKBLAZE_KEY_ID)`в”¬ГЂ
                    : \"(nenhuma credencial encontrada)\",в”¬ГЂ
                endpoint: process.env.BACKBLAZE_ENDPOINT || \"(default)\",в”¬ГЂ

              return NextResponse.json(в”¬ГЂ
                { errors: { form: \"Erro ao enviar documentos. Tente novamente.\" } },в”¬ГЂ
                { status: 503 },в”¬ГЂ
              );в”¬ГЂ
            }в”¬ГЂ
          }в”¬ГЂ
        }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
        // Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡ Gerar token Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡в”¬ГЂ

        // Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡ Encaminhar ao backend QWork Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡Г”Г¶Г‡в”¬ГЂ
        // QWORK_API_SKIP=true permite testar a LP localmente sem o backend QWork.в”¬ГЂ
        // Em produв”њВєв”њГєo, mantenha QWORK_API_SKIP indefinido ou false.в”¬ГЂ
        const skipQWork = process.env.QWORK_API_SKIP === \"true\";в”¬ГЂ
        const qworkUrl = process.env.QWORK_API_URL || \"http://localhost:3001\";в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ

              hasFiles,в”¬ГЂ

        } else {в”¬ГЂ
          // Mapeia campos camelCase da LP para snake_case esperado pelo QWorkв”¬ГЂ

          // Campos comunsв”¬ГЂ
          forwardData.append(\"tipo_pessoa\", (raw.tipoPessoa ?? \"\").toLowerCase());в”¬ГЂ
          forwardData.append(\"nome\", raw.nome ?? \"\");в”¬ГЂ
          forwardData.append(\"email\", raw.email ?? \"\");в”¬ГЂ
          forwardData.append(\"telefone\", raw.telefone ?? \"\");в”¬ГЂ
          forwardData.append(\"website\", \"\"); // honeypot vazioв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
          // Campos PFв”¬ГЂ
          if (raw.tipoPessoa === \"PF\") {в”¬ГЂ

            } else {в”¬ГЂ
              // DEV ou fallback (credenciais ausentes): repassa o arquivo para o QWork fazer o uploadв”¬ГЂ

            }в”¬ГЂ
          }в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
          // Campos PJв”¬ГЂ

            if (!qworkRes.ok) {в”¬ГЂ

              // Tentar parsear como JSON e extrair mensagem especв”њВЎficaв”¬ГЂ
              let qworkError: {в”¬ГЂ

              // Mapear erros de duplicaв”њВєв”њГєo para mensagens amigв”њГ­veisв”¬ГЂ
              let userMessage = \"Erro ao processar cadastro. Tente novamente.\";в”¬ГЂ
              let errorField: string | undefined;в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
              const isDuplicate =в”¬ГЂ
                qworkError.code === \"DUPLICATE\" ||в”¬ГЂ

                errorMsg.includes(\"duplicate\") ||в”¬ГЂ
                errorMsg.includes(\"в”њв•‘nico\") ||в”¬ГЂ
                errorMsg.includes(\"unico\") ||в”¬ГЂ
                errorMsg.includes(\"unique\") ||в”¬ГЂ
                errorMsg.includes(\"jв”њГ­ existe\") ||в”¬ГЂ
                errorMsg.includes(\"jв”њГ­ possui um cadastro\") ||в”¬ГЂ

                qworkError.field ??в”¬ГЂ
                (errorMsg.includes(\"cpf\")в”¬ГЂ
                  ? \"cpf\"в”¬ГЂ
                  : errorMsg.includes(\"cnpj\")в”¬ГЂ
                    ? \"cnpj\"в”¬ГЂ
                    : errorMsg.includes(\"email\")в”¬ГЂ
                      ? \"email\"в”¬ГЂ
                      : undefined);в”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂв”¬ГЂ
              if (isDuplicate && dupeField === \"cpf\") {в”¬ГЂ
                userMessage = \"Este CPF jв”њГ­ possui um cadastro em anв”њГ­lise.\";в”¬ГЂ
                errorField = \"cpf\";в”¬ГЂ
              } else if (isDuplicate && dupeField === \"cnpj\") {в”¬ГЂ
